  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

What you're describing is impossible. There's no way to save a Strigoi. When they're gone, they're gone. They're dead. Undead. Forever."<br />Robert's next words weren't directed at Adrian. They were spoken to me. "<i>That which is dead doesn't always stay dead....</i>"<br /><br /><b>After a long and heartbreaking journey to Siberia,</b> Dimitri’s birthplace, Rose Hathaway has finally returned to St. Vladimir’s—and to her best friend, Lissa Dragomir. It's graduation, and the girls can’t wait for their real lives outside the academy’s cold iron gates to finally begin. But even with the intrigue and excitement of court life looming, Rose’s heart still aches for Dimitri. He’s out there, somewhere.<br /><br />She failed to kill him when she had the chance, and now her worst fears are about to come true. Dimitri has tasted her blood, and she knows in her heart that he is hunting her. And if Rose won't join him, he won't rest until he has silenced her . . . <i>forever</i>.<br /><br />But Rose can't forget what she learned on her journey—whispers of a magic too impossible and terrifying to comprehend. A magic inextricably tied to Lissa that could hold the answer to all of Rose's prayers, but not without devastating consequences. Now Rose will have to decide what—and <i>who</i>—matters most to her. And in the end, is true love really worth the price?<br /><br />Fall in love with Rose and Dimitri all over again in <i>Spirit Bound</i>, the eagerly awaited fifth novel in Richelle Mead's enthralling <i>Vampire Academy</i> series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10128840845805828819" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

    They meet with Victor's brother, he is also a spirit user and if the silver stake can have a spirit charm and can be used by a spirit user (in this ca<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    They meet with Victor's brother, he is also a spirit user and if the silver stake can have a spirit charm and can be used by a spirit user (in this case Lissa) to awaken a strigoi from the dead. So Lissa stakes Dimitri which awakens him <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>

<div id="review_58327249" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/58327249" />
    <a title="Tatiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2250020-tatiana"><img alt="Tatiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1249783659p2/2250020.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/58327249?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tatiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tatiana" href="/user/show/2250020-tatiana">Tatiana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">I wouldn't</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2250020-tatiana?shelf=2010">2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2250020-tatiana?shelf=tres-annoying">tres-annoying</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2250020-tatiana?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2250020-tatiana?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2250020-tatiana?shelf=why-the-hype">why-the-hype</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer58327249" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16914508060439001736">This book is crap and Rose is a shameless gold-digging two-timer. <br/><br/>Yes-yes, I am in a minority here, but it won't be the first time, nor the last. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6479259.Spirit_Bound__Vampire_Academy___5_' title='Spirit Bound (Vampire Academy, #5) by Richelle Mead' rel='nofollow noopener'>Spirit Bound</a> is a bad book and I am contemplating to remove <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/137902.Richelle_Mead' title='Richelle Mead' rel='nofollow noopener'>Richelle Mead</a> from the list of the authors whose writing I care to follow. She can join my black list next to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1428675.Beth_Fantaskey' title='Beth Fantaskey' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beth Fantaskey</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/445303.Maria_V__Snyder' title='Maria V. Snyder' rel='nofollow noopener'>Maria V. Snyder</a>. I was willing to give VA another chance after the disappointment <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5996153.Blood_Promise__Vampire_Academy___4_' title='Blood Promise (Vampire Academy, #4) by Richelle Mead' rel='nofollow noopener'>Blood Promise</a> was, but no more, this series is taking its path into oblivion along </span>
  <span id="freeText16914508060439001736" style="display:none">This book is crap and Rose is a shameless gold-digging two-timer. <br /><br />Yes-yes, I am in a minority here, but it won't be the first time, nor the last. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6479259.Spirit_Bound__Vampire_Academy___5_" title="Spirit Bound (Vampire Academy, #5) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Spirit Bound</a> is a bad book and I am contemplating to remove <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/137902.Richelle_Mead" title="Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Richelle Mead</a> from the list of the authors whose writing I care to follow. She can join my black list next to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1428675.Beth_Fantaskey" title="Beth Fantaskey" rel="nofollow noopener">Beth Fantaskey</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/445303.Maria_V__Snyder" title="Maria V. Snyder" rel="nofollow noopener">Maria V. Snyder</a>. I was willing to give VA another chance after the disappointment <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5996153.Blood_Promise__Vampire_Academy___4_" title="Blood Promise (Vampire Academy, #4) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood Promise</a> was, but no more, this series is taking its path into oblivion along with Richelle's Georgina Kincaid books. Mead just can't produce this mediocre mess, destroy her characters for the sake of cheap relationship melodrama and contrived "love triangles" and expect me to eat it up. No, thanks.<br /><br />Now, for the good. We are back to the cast of characters we came to love in the first 3 books - Eddie, Mia, Christian (As I expected reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5996153.Blood_Promise__Vampire_Academy___4_" title="Blood Promise (Vampire Academy, #4) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood Promise</a>, almost none of the million characters introduced in it are back, they have served their filler purpose and now dead and gone). Lissa comes into her own powers and is an admirable person now. Lissa's and Christian's relationship is back on track, which is great because I still have no idea why they broke up in the first place.<br /><br />Now, for the bad. Where do I start? How about, the only feelings <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6479259.Spirit_Bound__Vampire_Academy___5_" title="Spirit Bound (Vampire Academy, #5) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Spirit Bound</a> was able to elicit in me were boredom and mild annoyance? <br /><br />It is surprising how a book so action-packed can be so thoroughly boring. A lot of things happen in it - Rose takes her final pre-graduation trials, she steals important prison files, she breaks into a maximum security vamp prison, then there is a final altercation with Dimitri. But just like in the latest installment of Mead's Georgina Kincaid series, these events are glossed over, everything happens without much effort, there is no tension build-up before each and every one of them, the characters don't experience too many obstacles and therefore there is no real feeling of something important happening.<br /><br />Also, the highest point of the book happens at about 300-page mark. What comes after is just added-on drama that comes out of nowhere (is Richelle paid per page?). I just can't believe that this kind of story is what Mead had pre-planned for the series (according to her, she plots her series in advance). If I knew that's the shape the series would take, I wouldn't have bothered to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/345627.Vampire_Academy__Vampire_Academy___1_" title="Vampire Academy (Vampire Academy, #1) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Vampire Academy</a>.<br /><br />Another thing. What kind of relationship do Rose and Adrian have? It's not only unhealthy, it's just wrong. What Mead has achieved with it is that now I am all on board with Rose/Adrian pairing in the end (I used to be a Team Dimitri girl), but not because I like Adrian now, but because they would make a mighty good couple: Rose can fantasize about Dimitri while blood-whoring with Adrian (he seems to be just fine with his status of sloppy seconds/doormat) and Adrian can get drunk, continue spending his daddy's money and drag Rose around to parties to get a kick out of his parents and get Rose humiliated by Moroi snobs. What a pair they make! <br /><br />Then there is Rose's inconsistent behavior (one minute she wants to kill Dimitri, another she will do anything to save him; one moment she is in love with Dimitri, another she is getting it on with Adrian), deus-ex machina (Mikhail anyone? how convenient!); redundant conversations; masked party (what was the point?); miraculous prison break, etc., etc...<br /> <br />I can go on and on with this tirade, but honestly, why? I think I am done with this series. For all I care, the entire cast of characters can die (well, they are sort of already dead to me due to the author's "skillful treatment") and I won't blink an eye. Why, oh why did I buy previous installments? There is no chance I will ever re-read them!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16914508060439001736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_95264263" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/95264263" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/95264263?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=the-great-shelf-of-meh">the-great-shelf-of-meh</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer95264263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8069142475912739953">The good news is this: Spirit Bound is better than Blood Promises.<br/><br/>Now let's all take a deep, satisfying breath of relief for that.<br/><br/>But, there is bad news. The character of Rose, for me, takes a huge hit in this installment. <br/><br/>Spirit Bound is fairly well written. The pacing is pretty good in that you don't have an opportunity to get bored. There are three points in the book that I really feel SHOULD have received far more attention and detail than they should:<br/><br/>Rose's exam, Victor's rescue (What shall</span>
  <span id="freeText8069142475912739953" style="display:none">The good news is this: Spirit Bound is better than Blood Promises.<br /><br />Now let's all take a deep, satisfying breath of relief for that.<br /><br />But, there is bad news. The character of Rose, for me, takes a huge hit in this installment. <br /><br />Spirit Bound is fairly well written. The pacing is pretty good in that you don't have an opportunity to get bored. There are three points in the book that I really feel SHOULD have received far more attention and detail than they should:<br /><br />Rose's exam, Victor's rescue (What shall be hereto referred to from now on as the stupidest act performed by Rose. Ever.) and the battle with Dimitri.<br /><br />There are many things in this book that I wish hadn't received quite so much attention, such as parties, family visits and general faffing about (To use another strange colloquialism)<br /><br />Despite that, the book is great - except I'd really like to strangle Rose. Really.<br /><br />I wouldn't necessarily consider myself Team Dimitri or Team Adrian. I may lean towards Adrian a little but her obsession for Dimitri makes me think that she's nowhere near good enough for him and therefor should stay with Dimitri AND DIE!<br /><br />How am I supposed to respect a heroine who uses her boyfriend's credit card to pay for her trip to Vegas with friends? Not to mention the money that she had already swindled from him to finance her little trip through Serbia! Then what was with her running around loudly declaring her love to Dimitri WHILE SHE IS SUPPOSED TO BE DATING ADRIAN?<br /><br />Seriously. I just wanted to smack her. <br /><br />Dimitri wasn't much better. As my little computer gaming brother would say - Less QQ and more PewPew. <br /><br />Other characters were awesome and well written. it ended on the most horrible cliff hanger and I'm considering starting a petition to make it illegal for authors to finish on such a very tense note!<br /><br />Over all, it's a a much better read than Blood Promises. There were aspects of this book that annoyed me but I really enjoyed reading it regardless and now I'm eagerly awaiting the sixth and final installment.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8069142475912739953" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_79130721" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/79130721" />
    <a title="Shelly Farez" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2866455-shelly-farez"><img alt="Shelly Farez" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1259353518p2/2866455.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/79130721?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelly Farez" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelly Farez" href="/user/show/2866455-shelly-farez">Shelly Farez</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer79130721" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7946703052823876334">heres for u people 2 enjoy found it<br/><br/><br/>Vampire Academy 5 - Spirit Bound<br/><br/>Author -- -- Richelle Mead<br/><br/>Chapter One<br/><br/>Lissa stared at the letter in shock. But not as much shock as me. I memorized the letter the Dimitri wrote me.<br/><br/>You forgot another lesson: Never turn your back until you know your enemy<br/><br/>is dead. Looks like we'll have to go over the lesson again the next time<br/><br/>I see you-which will be soon.<br/><br/>Love, D<br/><br/>The words were strapped into my head and they weren't moving anywhere. The words 'Which shall be soon' ke</span>
  <span id="freeText7946703052823876334" style="display:none">heres for u people 2 enjoy found it<br /><br /><br />Vampire Academy 5 - Spirit Bound<br /><br />Author -- -- Richelle Mead<br /><br />Chapter One<br /><br />Lissa stared at the letter in shock. But not as much shock as me. I memorized the letter the Dimitri wrote me.<br /><br />You forgot another lesson: Never turn your back until you know your enemy<br /><br />is dead. Looks like we'll have to go over the lesson again the next time<br /><br />I see you-which will be soon.<br /><br />Love, D<br /><br />The words were strapped into my head and they weren't moving anywhere. The words 'Which shall be soon' kept on running through my head. Like a fish that's stuck on a hook. I paced around the room frantically, hoping for something to come to my head. The stake was still in my hands and was starting to get really sweaty.<br /><br />"Rose! Are you even listening to me? I mean, what are we going to do!?" She was freaking more then me. "I don't want you to get hurt. Please. I need to help."<br /><br />Her words sunk into me. Giving me no choice but to bring her with me. My mind blew up with questions when my thought was decided. What if she got hurt? What about killed? What if her spirit starts to take over her again? What if starts to take over me? My head start to hurt. It isn't natural for a girl like me to think this much.<br /><br />"Rose!" She yelled in my face. "Talk. Let it out. Dont keep everything inside. I know you dont want me to control you're life, but you have had that same facial expression for almost 2 minutes straight and thats not normal," She pleaded. "You're scaring me."<br /><br />"Jeez, what are you? My therapist" I told her.<br /><br />She gave me a sincere smile since i changed my expression and spoke out loud. However, i still needed time to think, so i just sat on her bed and dug my face into my hands hoping for her to understand. Her response was to sit by me and wrap her arm around me. Close enough.<br /><br />I cant just bring Lissa alone. I would bring my mom. Maybe. But if i said even a word about leaving the academy again, she would lock me in my room. So mom is definitely off the list. Uhmmm, Christian? Nope, there fighting anyways and i do NOT want to lose my concentration if those two are arguing. Damn. I can think of anyone. I'll think of someone later.<br /><br />"Alright, Liss, you can come with me," I told her. "But, i don't want any questions about it right now. I'm still not even sure im going yet," Which i- we, probably are. "But for now, i think im going to stay at the academy."<br /><br />"Lissa's eyes flew up with a huge grin across her face like a 5 year old on Christmas morning. "Oh, Rose! You have no idea on how much i missed you!" She squealed<br /><br />"Alright Liss," I laughed. "I need to go and talk to Alberta and enroll into this hell school again."<br /><br />This going to just like when me and Lissa came back to St. Vladamir's before, except this time, I'm facing it alone. Right when i walked out of Lissa's door, eyes turned to me. Oh great, i thought to myself. And so it has begun.<br /><br />The walk to the office was totally akward. I saw some faces i knew stare at me. Like the girls that Lissa hung out with when she was going through her crazy phase with spirit. Then i saw Christian look at me like i was some ghost that came back from the grave. I mean, he was staring at me like when in movie some kid that randomly stares at you and then a second later they hit a wall or fall into a trash can, but no. There was no trash can. Making that expression stay on his face.<br /><br />But it wasn't just Christian, it was everyone. They were staring at me with same confused and surprised expression. Except for Mia. Mia was standing there with a grin slapped onto her face, she walked up to me, which everyone of her other friends were to scared to do.<br /><br />Mia's blond curls bounced as she walked toward me. Her grin was still placed on her face. Me and Mia have been on okay terms now ever since Mason died. I gues you could call us friends.<br /><br />"Hey Rose, havent seen you in a while," She smiled. "How has it been?"<br /><br />"Uhmm good?" Me and Mia may not hate each other, but that doesn't mean i like her enough to trust her.<br /><br />She just gave me one of her smiles and left. Guess she had nothing to start gossip about. Good, i thought.<br /><br />When i reached Alberta's, old but, again, new office, she was sitting in her desk reading something on her computer. When she looked up and saw me she waved me to come and sit down.<br /><br />"So Rose? Have you decieded yet?" She smiled at me.<br /><br />"Yup. I'm going to stay. But have you talked to anyone about putting me back in line to be Lissa's guardian?" I asked.<br /><br />"That's wonderful Rose," Then she smiled, and it wasn't one of her i-feel-bad-for-you smiles. "And yes, i have Rose. I see that you are wearing you're hair up today and almost everyone has noticed the marks on you're neck. After seeing how well you do, they have decided to give you're position as Lissa's guardian back. However, you must remain at the academy."<br /><br />"Really?! It was that easy!" I cheered. "Thank you SO much Alberta!"<br /><br />With that i walked out of the room. Then i saw the perfect person to take with Lissa and I at the end of the year. I walked up to him on put on my sly grin. He was already smiling before i even started to walk.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Spirit Bound -- chapter 2<br /><br />"Rose Hathaway is asking me, Adrian, to help assist her?" Adrian smirked.<br /><br />My smile was long gone by now and this converstation was really starting to turn out more annoything then i thought. "How many times do i have to go over this. You. Are. Coming. With. Me. And. Lissa. To. Kill. Dimitri."<br /><br />"Wait. I thought you told Alberta, that you;re staying until you graduate?" He questioned.<br /><br />"I am."<br /><br />"What if he gets here before you and Lissa graduate? He might bring a whole army by the sounds of what you did to him," He smirked.<br /><br />I ignored that second part not wanting to get the thought in my head. "You think i havent considered that? It's just that i cant make Lissa leave. Not now at least."<br /><br />"So, leave her behind."<br /><br />"This coming from the guy who was actually begging me to come back to Lissa because i left her."<br /><br />He didnt have a reply. Good, i thought.<br /><br />"Well, i said i would come," was his reply.<br /><br />"Uhmm, no. No, you didnt say anything, yet," I smirked with a wink. That outta' get his attention.<br /><br />"Hmm," He started. "I guess that queen Tatina wouldnt mind a responsible adult taking care of her apperntice, So, i guess i should come."<br /><br />"You? Responsible? Thats rich," I laughed. "But good. You're a go." Lets just hope Dimitri doesnt come before then.<br /><br />He just smiled, excused himself and went to go find Lissa for there sunday lessons. Since i was going to be doing things like i used to, before i left i thought i should go to church. For old times sake.<br /><br />The walk to the chapel was worse to the walk to Albertas office. Maybe i should go to my room, i thought. No. Im going to have to have to face this sooner or later, and sooner is way better. People were going to ask how my journey went, so instead of telling them i tied up my hair into a bun showing my marks. The second my mark was visible, i heard people gasp. Jeez, wannabes, i thought to myself.<br /><br />"When i finally reached the church, there was a new priest. Yet somehow, he knew me. "Rose Hathaway," he smiled. "It is a pleasure to meet you. I am Father Shay, please sit down."<br /><br />What happened to the other guy? He was pretty old, but i'll miss him. He gave me the first clue with Lissa and her powers and out bond.<br /><br />I forgot how boring curch was when Father Shay started talking. I remember why i went to church before, to see Lissa. And only Lissa. After another 10 minutes i just tuned my self out.<br /><br />The thing finished about an hour later. I nearly ran out of the chapel, happy to smell the fresh air not some strong vinegar type scent that the priest calls 'holy water'. The air was cool and moist, just the way it was in Russia. THat reminded me, I should call the Belikovs soon to let them know im okay. I might even call Abe because of the good mood im in.<br /><br />I walked back to the dorm, more eyes then before for some strange reason. People were still gasping and making a big fuss over my marks. I thankfully saw Lissa and ran over to her.<br /><br />"Lissa! Lissa!" I yelled at her. "Wait for a second."<br /><br />Not that she needed to, i could catch up to her easily as a dhaphir.<br /><br />"Rose! How was church?" She laughed.<br /><br />I shot her the look of death, she remembered how much i hated church. Even though i forgot. "You know how much i hate church." I shot back at her.<br /><br />"Then why would you go?" She mused.<br /><br />"I dont know! People were staring and i saw the chapel and the old priest was so nice- what happened to him anyways?" Curiosity popped in my head again.<br /><br />"Rose, he was almost a 100 years old," Those eyes were deep and full of sorrow. "And get this, the new preist is only human. He's not a moroi or dhampir or anyhing. Just human."<br /><br />Thats strange, i thought. Why would the academy higher a human priest? Why would a human priest want to talk about history thats not even from his own race? Why would he even want to talk about any history? Liss, probably missed the priest more then me. He helped us so much before we knew about spirit and when she was in the chapel but not in the attic, he would help her inderstand her powers from what he knew.<br /><br />"That is strange, but he seemed nice enough," I said. "Probably to scared to say anything to us."<br /><br />She laughed and rolled her eyes, " Probably."<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7946703052823876334" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText11542429118991369466" style="display:none">Spirit Bound (Vampire Academy, #5), Richelle Mead <br /><br />First Publication date: May 18, 2010. The book starts off with Rose reading the last in a series of love letters/death threats from Dimitri. <br /><br />The final exams are set to start in short time and she resolves to stay focused and pass them to the best of her abilities and hope it will be enough for her to get assigned to Lissa. <br /><br />The teachers test her by having her trapped on a swinging bridge with Strigoi approaching on both sides, which she passes by cutting the bridge, then "killing" the opponents on her end. <br /><br />After Abe's network relayed a message from Victor Dashkov that there was nothing he could be bribed with while he was behind bars, Rose plots with Lissa and Eddie to break him out of his high security vampire prison. <br /><br />They successfully do so by disguising themselves as guardians bringing new feeders and relying heavily on Lissa's compulsion abilities. Victor agrees to lead them to his brother, Robert, a reclusive spirit user who is rumored to have once returned a Strigoi to their original state. <br /><br />They travel to Las Vegas, where Adrian tracks Rose's credit cards and follows them. While not very pleased with Rose's continued endeavors to help Dimitri, he stays with them. <br /><br />Robert tells them that the Spirit user must infuse a stake with Spirit and kill the Strigoi on its own, but escapes when they are attacked by Dimitri and other Strigoi. <br /><br />They manage to escape and upon their arrival at court Eddie and Rose are punished for endangering the Moroi and sent to do physical labor. While they are occupied, Lissa and Christian are kidnapped by Dimitri as bait for Rose. ...<br /><br />تاریخ نخستین خوانش: روز نوزدهم ماه سپتامبر سال 2017 میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: پیمان روح: کتاب پنجم از سری: آکادمی خون آشام؛ نویسنده ریچل مید؛ ژانر فانتزی، رومنس، خون آشامی؛ در 321ص؛ <br /><br />چکیده داستان: پس از یک سفر طولانی و ناامید کننده به محل تولد «دیمیتری» در سیبری، «رز هاتاوی» بالاخره به نزد بهترین دوستش «لیسا» برگشت؛ تا فارغ التحصیلی چیزی نمانده، و آنها منتظر زندگی واقعی پشت دروازه های آهنین آکادمی هستند؛ اما قلب «رز» هنوز در پیش «دیمیتری» است که میداند جایی آن بیرون است؛ این کتاب پنجمین کتاب سری فانتزی «آکادمی خون‌آشام» است؛ «ریچل مید» پیش از آنکه به نویسندگی بپردازد، در سه رشته تحصیل کرد و به عنوان مربی راهنمایی مشغول به کار بود؛ او سرانجام به این نتیجه رسید که راه خود را در نویسندگی ادامه دهد، ایشان باور دارند که تحصیلاتش، ایشان را برای این کار آماده کرد<br /><br />تاریخ بهنگام رسانی 22/04/1399هجری خورشیدی؛ ا. شربیانی</span>

<div id="review_73613563" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/73613563" />
    <a title="Sarah Jo." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2661598-sarah-jo"><img alt="Sarah Jo." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396480887p2/2661598.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/73613563?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah Jo." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah Jo." href="/user/show/2661598-sarah-jo">Sarah Jo.</a>
      </span>

        rated it

Suddenly, I had a new perspective when it comes to reading.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434030077ra/15169303.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402272468ra/9915252.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I discovered book characters that got under my skin like no others before.<br>And the plot... it was so interesting I just had to know what was going to happen'.<br>I had to know how Rose and Dimitri will resolve what was going on between them, what will be with Vasilisa and Christian... and him... <br>For the first time in my life, I fell in love with the book character: Adrian Ivashkov.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450718251ra/17459588.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't have to say it: My life was never the same again!<br><br>And the best part: realization that there are countless worlds that I have yet to discover, many characters that are waiting for me to hang out with them, zillion adventures that I still have to go on.<br><br><b>...and that is how my love for YA genre began.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433593768ra/15117107.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41973734-merphy-napier?shelf=three-stars">three-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41973734-merphy-napier?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2756602064" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer538842748655710805">Enjoyment level was probably around a 2.5 but I think that's in large part just that this series isn't for me anymore. I think it's more like a 3.5<br/><br/>Things this series does well:<br/>- world building. The different types of vampires are so interesting and well built<br/>- magic. I LOVE the different types of magic these vampires and wield <br/>- politics. The political moves are very interesting and well done<br/><br/>Things I don't love:<br/>- writing. I don't like nitpicking writing but I know some people care about this. Th</span>
  <span id="freeText538842748655710805" style="display:none">Enjoyment level was probably around a 2.5 but I think that's in large part just that this series isn't for me anymore. I think it's more like a 3.5<br /><br />Things this series does well:<br />- world building. The different types of vampires are so interesting and well built<br />- magic. I LOVE the different types of magic these vampires and wield <br />- politics. The political moves are very interesting and well done<br /><br />Things I don't love:<br />- writing. I don't like nitpicking writing but I know some people care about this. The number of times a character "exclaimed" something rather than yelling, or calling out, or shouting, etc was... a lot. There were a lot of simple thins like that that I know would bother a lot of readers.<br />- relationships. I really don't know that there's a healthy relationship situation Rose gets into. Power imbalances, "lust charms" that force characters into sexual situations, etc, it all makes it difficult for me to really "ship" anyone<br />- rose. I wanna love rose but I have a rough time with her. She nonstop makes terrible, impulsive, and stupid decisions in the name of what's right. It's stated on paper that this is a fault of hers, but this deep into the series I'd *really* like to see some growth.<br /><br />Anyway, I know i'm close to the end of the series but I just really don't think it's the right books for me anymore, so I think this'll be the last one for me &lt;3</span>

<div id="review_2188589980" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2188589980" />
    <a title="Fuzaila" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/55299343-fuzaila"><img alt="Fuzaila" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532881347p2/55299343.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2188589980?book_show_action=true">Nov 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fuzaila" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fuzaila" href="/user/show/55299343-fuzaila">Fuzaila</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55299343-fuzaila?shelf=books-in-series">books-in-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55299343-fuzaila?shelf=horror-paranormal">horror-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55299343-fuzaila?shelf=romance-lovey-dovey">romance-lovey-dovey</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55299343-fuzaila?shelf=made-me-lol">made-me-lol</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55299343-fuzaila?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55299343-fuzaila?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55299343-fuzaila?shelf=liked-it-but-i-am-not-sure">liked-it-but-i-am-not-sure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55299343-fuzaila?shelf=suspense-thriller-mystery">suspense-thriller-mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55299343-fuzaila?shelf=characters-that-hold-my-heart">characters-that-hold-my-heart</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2188589980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12132205223145647050"><b>What is this book?</b> I was planning on ditching it up until 80% of it, and in a bizarre turn of events, I lost a night to this book and jumped onto the sequel right after <s>wtf I blame this book for making me a messy insomniac</s>.?<b> That’s extraordinary. </b>Not that this book was any good. Richelle Mead is one manipulative author. Like <i>really, really manipulative.</i> How dare she light my heart with fury like that and become the fireman all of a sudden? Ugh, this one’s going to be hard to review, not to menti</span>
  <span id="freeText12132205223145647050" style="display:none"><b>What is this book?</b> I was planning on ditching it up until 80% of it, and in a bizarre turn of events, I lost a night to this book and jumped onto the sequel right after <s>wtf I blame this book for making me a messy insomniac</s>.?<b> That’s extraordinary. </b>Not that this book was any good. Richelle Mead is one manipulative author. Like <i>really, really manipulative.</i> How dare she light my heart with fury like that and become the fireman all of a sudden? Ugh, this one’s going to be hard to review, not to mention rate. <br /><br />First half of the book? <b>1/5 stars</b> <br />The 60%-80% potion of the book? <b>3/5 stars</b> <br />That ending though? <b>4.5/5 stars</b> <br /><br />Overall, <b>2.5/5 stars</b><br /><br /><b>**As always, please be aware of spoilers in case you have not read the previous books**</b><br /><br /><br /><s>
  <u>
    <b>THE PLOT</b>
  </u>
</s><br /><br />Let’s say um, where did that previous book end? I am not so sure. But this one started quite sometime after. <br />Rose and Adrian are dating. Yeah, finally. But she is not very sure of her feelings for him. She is <b>
  <i>confused</i>
</b>. Because, duh, her ex-boyfriend is dead (undead-whatever) and might have a shot at being bought to life which would mean busting a notorious criminal out from his high-security prison. So what does <i>
  <b>invincible, reckless, i-am-in-control-of-everything</b>
</i> Rose do? She emotionally manipulates, Lissa, her best friend, who thinks she owes her, in coming with her to bust that monster out and try to regain a Strigoi, which might not even be possible. In doing so, they are risking the entire Vampire world, Rose and Lissa’s future, the love and life of everyone they hold dear, to accomplish what? <b>To bring a dead man out alive because Rose loved him.</b> (Raise your hands if you didn’t cringe at that?)<br /><br />Anyways, Miracles do happen and it happens here, but one problem leads to another, and in the end, Rose finds herself tackled in a web of conspiracies and an impossible quest; she isn’t even sure how she got herself there, or even worse, how she’d ever be able to get herself out. <br /><br /><b><u>MY THOUGHTS</u> </b><s>more like, my tangled chain of emotions</s><br /><br />•	Let’s be real and admit this: <b>Rose is the most annoying, whiny, emotionally manipulative, utterly-selfish, reckless brat who does EVERYTHING with selfish notions <s>and regrets every bit of her recklessness later<s></s></s></b>. Like, for most part of this book, I ABSOLUTELY HATED HER. In fact, I can’t even remember an instant when she was bearable. She was awful to those who loved her, using them to get her way in and out of things, and not even giving a second thought on how much her actions might affect them. <br /><br />•	Btw, the way she described her love-life. <b>Disgusting.</b> It was as if the only good thing about being in love was the kisses, cuddles and sex. <br /><br />•	<b>I DON’T SHIP ROSE AND DIMITRI.</b> There – I say it again and I will say this all the time. I didn’t see any development in their relationship. I don’t even think they make a good pair. Because, honestly, Dimitri and Rose are the most annoying MCs I’ve read yet. Oh, Heck. They make the best pair. They are perfect for each other.<br /><br />•	But darn, Rose, why do you hurt my baby Adrian so much??? You know you aren’t going to stick around when Dimitri is back and yet you stay in hopes of comforting him. <b>Are you crazy???</b> You don’t get to control everybody’s mind by just being there!!! <br /><br />•	Oh, sorry, I totally forgot. She IS crazy.<br /><br />•	<b>Lissa</b> has to be the best thing to happen in this book. Her character development was remarkable. I loved her better than Rose, but still, it’s not completely enough.<br /> <br />•	Likewise, I LOVE CHRISTIAN’s character. Amazing. Bold. Ready-for-action. Cool. Just right for Lissa. <br /><br />•	And not to mention, Adrian. How could he be such a bundle of pitiful-cutie-pie? I hate that he is still bowled over by Rose, but nevertheless. HE IS AMAZING.<br /><br />•	The thing is, Mead doesn’t give much thought to her side-characters. The whole thing is just about Rose, Rose and Rose. Plus Dimitri (thankfully, not as much as in the last book though)<br /><br />•	If she had given Adrian, Lissa, Christian and some others, a fair chance, a bit more role, development, this book would have been so much better. Where is Jill btw?<br /><br />•	Another thing about Rose that I hate – the whole book might be about her – but it is impossible how she gets her way ALL THE DAMN TIME. Come on! She’s barely adult, she is stupid even. There is no explanation as to how those ‘ideas’ come to her. Everything seems way too <i>convenient</i> for her and it’s unrealistic how EVERYTHING <i>happens in her favor.</i><br /><br />•	Be reasonable Mead, you don’t have to go out of the way to make us like Rose. It can’t be always her. She’s the heroine of the story, true. Doesn’t mean there’s no other person who’s a hero too. Doesn’t have to be Rose all the time.<br /><br />•	Like, people have turned Strigoi for centuries now and they’ve earned the title as evil-creatures-of-the-night. But when Rose’s so-called-soulmate turns into one, there suddenly appears to be a way to restore them back to human? Ofcourse, MIRACLE. Duh. So simple.<br /><br />• And I’m now going to address another important but highly overlooked issue here - <b>MONEY</b> Yeah I know, it might be the least of your concerns, but really, the way money is made out to be the most commonly available thing ever? It’s offending. Rose is rich by no means, but she says she is funded by Adrian who is royal, but come one! Even Royals have their limit! Living in luxurious hotels and flying to some country every other minute? It’s not just costly, IT IS SUPER EXPENSIVE. How can anyone not see that? From the way Mead writes it, Rose might sctuslly be walking over a carpet of money. IT. IS. INSANE. THE AMOUNT OF MONEY – NOT HERS – SHE SPENDS.<br /><br />•	I’ve said this once, (twice? Idk), the plot is as repetitive as it can get. It is always the same thing over and over again. Someone gets kidnapped. Mostly Lissa. Rose leads a group of guardians to them. They emerge victorious. End of story. Happily Ever After. Cool.<br /><br /><br /><b>Overall,</b> this book was way too long for what good it did to the series. The plot is repetitive, but the ending came as a total surprise even when I was spoiled on the book’s happenings. I love the action part though, not too confusing, just enough to grip you on edge. But it’s still annoying – this technique of Mead to write horribly for most of the book and finally grab us with the endings. No one’s complaining tbh.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12132205223145647050" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <b>"I've given up on you... Love fades. Mine has."</b>
</i><br/><br/>This fifth installment of the Vampire Academy did surprise me. It has a boring and slow start, but when I got into the middle part of it, I was dumbstrucked with all its epicness.<br/><br/>I could not say much about the plot since it will spoil those who haven't yet read this, but the pacing became better.   <span id="freeText5566958963315757765" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"I've given up on you... Love fades. Mine has."</b>
</i><br /><br />This fifth installment of the Vampire Academy did surprise me. It has a boring and slow start, but when I got into the middle part of it, I was dumbstrucked with all its epicness.<br /><br />I could not say much about the plot since it will spoil those who haven't yet read this, but the pacing became better. There were more surprising things in the second half of it. Mostly I was stunned by the turn of events-- including that plot twist at the end!<br /><br />Rose was quite annoying in this book. I couldn't deny the fact that I was irritated by her immaturity here but thankfully, her character became better at the final chapters.<br /><br />I could never express how I love this series. Seriously, it becomes more and more incredible in each sequel. The final book will surely be a blast!<br /><br />Rating: 5 Stars</span>

<div id="review_73995313" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/73995313" />
    <a title="Heather" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2098381-heather"><img alt="Heather" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474068564p2/2098381.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/73995313?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather" href="/user/show/2098381-heather">Heather</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2098381-heather?shelf=2010">2010</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer73995313" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3389544675777338954">I did it. I know I said that I wouldn’t, but I read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6479259.Spirit_Bound__Vampire_Academy___5_' title='Spirit Bound (Vampire Academy, #5) by Richelle Mead' rel='nofollow noopener'>Spirit Bound</a> in spite of my boycott. I have no excuse. I’m almost as big a hypocrite as Rose Hathaway. Almost. In my defense, I didn’t decide to read it until after I read every spoiler available via Amazon.com. Therefore, I knew every plot point within this book before I read it, and ironically, it was the very thing that compelled me to read it. Curse my morbid curiosity. Worse, I liked it! I may never forgive myself.<br/>Before I say anything els</span>
  <span id="freeText3389544675777338954" style="display:none">I did it. I know I said that I wouldn’t, but I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6479259.Spirit_Bound__Vampire_Academy___5_" title="Spirit Bound (Vampire Academy, #5) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Spirit Bound</a> in spite of my boycott. I have no excuse. I’m almost as big a hypocrite as Rose Hathaway. Almost. In my defense, I didn’t decide to read it until after I read every spoiler available via Amazon.com. Therefore, I knew every plot point within this book before I read it, and ironically, it was the very thing that compelled me to read it. Curse my morbid curiosity. Worse, I liked it! I may never forgive myself.<br />Before I say anything else, I have to state this officially, for the review record…I HATE Rose. HATE her. I have resigned myself to the fact that we shall never, ever see any character growth from her, if anything, we can expect consistent digression, but still, this knowledge does not make me hate her any less. She is whinny, self involved, selfish, brash, manipulative, dishonest, and hypocritical. My favorite line to hate from her appears several times throughout this novel…”It was hard, but I pushed the guilt aside.” Hold the phone; I’m supposed to feel sorry for you because you are somehow able to overcome your guilt about destroying the lives of the people who love you while you get innocent people killed for your own selfish gains? Not likely. Even worse, I think I actually saw red while reading Rose's flippant, often condesending treatment of Adrian. Rose doesn’t deserve any of the people who love her, not Lissa, not Adrian, not Christian, Eddie, or the help or respect of any of the people that assist her on her journey. The only reason I root for her is because not rooting for her would be a betrayal to the characters I do love, namely Adrian, Lissa and Christian.<br /><br />Any of those who know my thoughts on this series know I am team Adrian through and through. He appears morally ambiguous upon first glance, when in fact; I think he may have the strongest moral character of any of them. He may drink and smoke like a freight train. He may even be a bit of a sloth, but there isn’t anything he wouldn’t do for the people he loves, even to his own detriment. His willingness to help maybe self motivated, but he has never ever operated under false pretenses, has never lied and never manipulated those he claims to love. Because I love Adrian, I want him to have that which he desires most, Rose. And I was so glad that he has finally been given the opportunity to have her. However, that does not mean that I think he should end up with her. Though for Adrian’s sake I hoped for the pairing, I have always known, and know, that Rose and Dimitri will end up together, as they should. Rose doesn’t deserve Adrian on her best day. Let's face it, I don't even think she deserves Dimtri. But I am so glad that Mead gave Adrian a chance to shine. And this fact along with two others is the only reason I liked this book and broke my vow to not read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6479259.Spirit_Bound__Vampire_Academy___5_" title="Spirit Bound (Vampire Academy, #5) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Spirit Bound</a>. I can turn my back on Rose, but I could never turn my back on Adrian.<br /><br />Thankfully, Mead also decided to devote more page time not only to Adrian, but to Lissa and Christian as well. These characters are so full of win in this installment that they somehow allowed me to overlook my hatred for Rose. That is a tremendous testament to their awesomeness. I know many people resent Lissa, though I have never understood why, she has always proven her friendship and loyalty to Rose, if anything, I’ve always felt that Rose had something to prove, but once again, Lissa outshines Rose in every way and puts her to extreme shame. <br />*Spoilers Ahead*. <br />I was proud of Lissa for restoring Dimitri, not because I felt that she owed it to Rose, but because if showed Lissa’s immense, all consuming selflessness, as well as her development in the use of Spirit. Lissa is just awesome, in an angelic sort of way. And Christian, oh how I missed him in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5996153.Blood_Promise__Vampire_Academy___4_" title="Blood Promise (Vampire Academy, #4) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood Promise</a>. Thankfully, he is back on par with his snide antics, shrewd observations, and endless love for Lissa, which is filled with that delicious tension that makes your stomach clench. I ate it up.<br /><br />As for Dimitri, I have never really liked or disliked him, except in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5996153.Blood_Promise__Vampire_Academy___4_" title="Blood Promise (Vampire Academy, #4) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood Promise</a>. I clearly disliked Strigoi Dimitri. He was such a forgone cliché as a Strigoi. Nevertheless, I am glad his humanity was restored and even better, he upped the angst ante with his rejection of Rose. Mead may be brilliant at destroying her characters (Seth from Georgia Kincaid series anyone?) as she has proven with Rose, but you can’t deny her ability to rip your heart out. I don’t even really care if Rose gets her happy ending, in fact, I hope she meets a tragic end in the last installment, but even I was in a state over Dimitri’s words in the church. Oh the angst! Rose and Dimitri belong together, even though it makes me kind of sick. I can't help but want it to happen, for Dimitri's sake.<br /><br />So Mead has redeemed herself a bit in my eyes. I may despise Rose with a fiery passion, but she knocked one out of the park by allowing Adrian and Lissa to surpass the narrator and steal the show and for peppering this book with so much emotional turmoil, deceit, tension and steam, that I couldn’t help but read it and like it. Kudos.<br /><br />P.S. If Mead turns Adrain into any more of a sacraficial lamb I will be truly devestated. Give the man a break for Christ's sake, he's been through enough already.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3389544675777338954" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText3305399051921325816" style="display:none"><u>4.5 Miracle ★'s</u><br><br><i>“As he looked at me, he seemed to send a message of his own: that he would still fight for me, that he would fight until he collapsed to keep them from taking me.”</i><br><br>Wow. Who just so happens to be Victor Dashkov's half-brother. So Rose formulates a plan to break Victor out of Tarasov prison. Consequences be damned. She recruits Mikhail Tanner (lover of Sonya Karp) to help get her, Lissa and Eddie out of the Academy. I love Eddie and his loyalty to his friends but I wish he wouldn't take so many risks with his promising future. Anyways after the prison break, they meet up with Robert in Las Vagus. They learn it's true, you can indeed restore a Strigoi but it's not so easy. You must use a stake charmed with Spirit and it must be used by a Spirit user in order for it to work. I love that this also brings Lissa and Christian back together. They have a common goal. Learn how to Stake a Strigoi!<br><br>When Lissa and Christian are on there way back from the Royal Court to the Academy they are attacked by Strigoi. She turns to Adrian. But Rose isn't going to give up. Quitting isn't in her blood. <br><br>Then at the end, Rose is arrested for "supposedly" killing the Queen Tatiana Marina Ivashkov. <br>She gets handed a letter from Ambrose. <br>Before her death, Tatiana wrote a letter to Rose and this is what it said.<br><br>Rose,<br>If you're reading this, then something terrible has happened. You probably hate me, and I don't blame you. I can only ask that you trust that what I did with the age decree was better for your people than what others had planned. There are some Moroi who want to force all dhampirs into service, whether they want it or not, by using compulsion. The age decree has slowed that faction down. However, I write to you with a secret you must put right, and it is a secret you must share with as few as possible. Vasilisa needs her spot on the Council, and it can be done. She is not the last Dragomir. Another lives, the illegitimate child of Eric Dragomir. I know nothing else, but if you can find this son or daughter, you will give Vasilisa the power she deserves. No matter your faults and dangerous temperament, you are the only one I feel can take on this task.     <a title="Rachel (The Rest Is Still Unwritten)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2406353-rachel-the-rest-is-still-unwritten"><img alt="Rachel (The Rest Is Still Unwritten)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305870184p2/2406353.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/59236454?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel (The Rest Is Still Unwritten)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel (The Rest Is Still Unwritten)" href="/user/show/2406353-rachel-the-rest-is-still-unwritten">Rachel (The Rest Is Still Unwritten)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2406353-rachel-the-rest-is-still-unwritten?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2406353-rachel-the-rest-is-still-unwritten?shelf=i-own">i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2406353-rachel-the-rest-is-still-unwritten?shelf=bought-by-me">bought-by-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer59236454&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer59236454" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7958378872969701478">***OMG, OMG, OMG! Ahhhhhh!!!!!!!****<br/>*sigh*<br/>Now that that’s out of the way, let’s move on....<br/>That was incredible. Just incredible! I cannot believe all that went on in that book.<br/>Firstly, Dimitri was saved! Yes, yes, yes! I can’t be happier about that, I swear. I actually shrieked when I read Lissa had actually managed to restore his soul. Let’s face it- it’s what every VA fan has wanted since the end of Shadow Kiss. And I’m no exception. <br/>My heart breaks over the guilt he feels and I know he can’t </span>
  <span id="freeText7958378872969701478" style="display:none">***OMG, OMG, OMG! Ahhhhhh!!!!!!!****<br />*sigh*<br />Now that that’s out of the way, let’s move on....<br />That was incredible. Just incredible! I cannot believe all that went on in that book.<br />Firstly, Dimitri was saved! Yes, yes, yes! I can’t be happier about that, I swear. I actually shrieked when I read Lissa had actually managed to restore his soul. Let’s face it- it’s what every VA fan has wanted since the end of Shadow Kiss. And I’m no exception. <br />My heart breaks over the guilt he feels and I know he can’t take back the things he’s done, but surely he can move on. And what about him not wanting to be with Rose? I understand how bad knowing he’d hurt the person he loves most would be, but there is NO WAY I believe he no longer loves her. That’s an outright lie! You only have to read how he looks at her and how he was willing to fight a bunch of guardians for her. He aint fooling anybody! <br />Oh, Rose. Dearest Rose..... WHAT ARE YOU DOING? She loves Dimka, that’s clear, but what about Adrian? I know her feelings are confused, especially knowing she does care about Adrian, but she is only going to make things harder on herself. And on Adrian if she does end up getting back with Dimitri. I believe Adrian does actually love her and his heart will break if they split.<br />That being said, I wouldn’t be true to myself or honest if I didn’t say that even though I have a soft spot for Adrian, I’ll be cheering for Rose and Dimitri all the way to the very end.<br />Lissa and Christian seemed to work things out, which was great to see. And many of the other awesome characters I love were back. Eddie, Abe, Mia, Rose’s Mum, Jill, even Sydney had a small cameo. It was soooo great to see them all again!<br /><br />Now on to the shocks! How can they believe that Rose killed the Queen? It’s an exceptional twist in the story, but I do wonder who actually did kill her and why? Now that Rose is going to trial it’s gonna be up to Lissa and all her friends to save her and get her out of trouble.<br />And Lissa has a sibling! Can you believe it? That totally blew me away, and I never saw it coming. I can’t wait to find out how that impacts the storyline. Even though it’s a surprise, I think a younger sis or bro would be good for Lissa. It means she’s not as alone as she’s always been. <br /><br />I CANNOT WAIT to find out what happens in the final book. I’m sad that Last Sacrifice will be the end of the VA series, but I’m looking forward to what I know will be a gripping, explosive, heart racing conclusion.<br />Now I just gotta wait until December. Seriously, it’s gonna kill me!!!<br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_134550060" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/134550060" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1489224-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1338449051p2/1489224.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/134550060?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/1489224-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1489224-lisa?shelf=paranormal-romance-urban-fantasy">paranormal-romance-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1489224-lisa?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer134550060" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18385246157983942568">Since a large part of this review is dedicated to my hatred of the romances in this series, I'll start by saying I never liked Rose and Dimitri together because I never understood why they liked each other. Richelle Mead <b>told</b> us that Dimitri and Rose were alike and that's why they were soul mates but she never <b>showed</b> that in the writing. How is Dimitri at all like Rose? Other than fighting, wanting to protect Moroi, and being in love with Rose, which are three things that apply to almost every m</span>
  <span id="freeText18385246157983942568" style="display:none">Since a large part of this review is dedicated to my hatred of the romances in this series, I'll start by saying I never liked Rose and Dimitri together because I never understood why they liked each other. Richelle Mead <b>told</b> us that Dimitri and Rose were alike and that's why they were soul mates but she never <b>showed</b> that in the writing. How is Dimitri at all like Rose? Other than fighting, wanting to protect Moroi, and being in love with Rose, which are three things that apply to almost every male guardian in this book, they have nothing in common. Also, I have to admit that I was uncomfortable with their relationship because he was her teacher, but I might have been able to overlook that if they had been written better and if I had liked Dimitri more.<br /><br />I agree with others that despite all of the action, this book was slow and boring. Everything was too easy and the plot was very contrived. Why did Victor need Lissa in the first book if his brother was a Spirit user? Eddie just does whatever Rose says because he trusts her and then conveniently goes missing for the rest of the book once he's served his purpose. Someone needs to remind me why Adrian is in love with Rose. I think they have good chemistry at times but it's impossible to root for them when she treats him like crap and uses him constantly.<br /><br />And I'll reiterate what I said in my review of Blood Promise, the love triangle was completely useless because it's completely obvious who Rose is going to end up with. Mead, who is clearly in love with Dimitri the same way Stephenie Meyer is in love with Edward, can't let Rose have real feelings for Adrian and move on with him. That would have created tension and added complexity to Rose's feelings. In real life people can have meaningful relationships with more than one person (just not at the same time) without diminishing the the love felt for either partner. If Rose had moved on with Adrian it would have also explained why he would stick around when her feelings began to waver since he would have had something real to miss and want to hold on to.<br /><br />But all of the problems with this book are common to books that star Mary Sues. Rose has been a Mary Sue from the beginning but at least there were consequences to her actions some of the time and she had faults that the characters in the book acknowledged. By Spirit Bound, the consequences she faced were not in response to things she should have been punished for. She's not punished for her selfish behavior regarding Dimitri or Adrian. Adrian forgives her for using him and Dimitri rejects her to protect her, not because of the means she used to save him or because he realizes what a selfish person she is. Nor is she punished for letting loose an evil man who hurt her best friend. She has to file papers for a few days for sneaking out, hardly the appropriate punishment for what she actually did. The only consequence she really faced was in response to her rightfully speaking out against the Queen for lowering the guardian age and that was only a small part of why she was accused of murder. Most of it was because she was framed.<br /><br />Honestly, I wouldn't continue reading this series except that I have a masochistic need to finish a series that I've started.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18385246157983942568" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/94655208" />
    <a title="Janina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3455554-janina"><img alt="Janina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1404584313p2/3455554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/94655208?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Janina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Janina" href="/user/show/3455554-janina">Janina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780141331874" href="/book/show/7694286-spirit-bound">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3455554-janina?shelf=young-adult-fiction">young-adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3455554-janina?shelf=given-away">given-away</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3455554-janina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3455554-janina?shelf=abandoned">abandoned</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer94655208" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2846596885044297892">Again, I found this book a bit too long-winded and I have to admit that I skimmed through quite a few pages. Especially the 'action' parts were a little bit boring. Some problems were solved in a rather easy way (the break-in into the guardians' headquarters, for example) and there wasn't one scene when I felt like the life of one of the 'important' characters was at stake. <br/>The relationship-focused parts of the story made up for that a little bit, although Rose's behaviour around Adrian made me </span>
  <span id="freeText2846596885044297892" style="display:none">Again, I found this book a bit too long-winded and I have to admit that I skimmed through quite a few pages. Especially the 'action' parts were a little bit boring. Some problems were solved in a rather easy way (the break-in into the guardians' headquarters, for example) and there wasn't one scene when I felt like the life of one of the 'important' characters was at stake. <br />The relationship-focused parts of the story made up for that a little bit, although Rose's behaviour around Adrian made me very angry. She tells him she is ready to move on, but nevertheless thinks mostly of Dimitri when they are together. I found that extremely mean, but couldn't understand why Adrian let himself be used as her doormat at the same time. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I really think this series could have redeemed itself had Mead had the guts to kill Dimitri off in the last book. But alas, there is no real chance for Rose and Adrian, which makes the whole love triangle completely meaningless. We all know who Rose will end up with. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />All in all, I have to say that I'm quite disappointed at how this series is developing. The last two books could have easily been shortened into one. I think I read only two thirds of this one without skimming, and I don't feel like I missed something important at all. Additionally, Mead's way of retelling what happened previously has begun to annoy me. I've never had problems with that in her Succubus series, but here it feels forced and disturbes the flow of her writing. Also, I always feel a little stupid as a reader when an author thinks she has to repeat everything for me. I know I'm forgetful, but not that much that I need every little fact shoved in my face again.<br /><br />Nevertheless, I'm still curious how this all will end, so I will probably read the last installment.<br /><br /><i>Edit: After reading a few spoiler reviews on 'Last Sacrifice', I have decided not to read the last book after all. I just can't take Rose's behaviour anymore. Sad that this series went downhill after book three.</i></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>,

<span id="freeTextContainer17554750190816976721">Wow!!! Just wow!! I can now say with certainty that Vampire Academy has just become <i>the</i> classic example of why great books should not be allowed to become series. <b>Spirit Bound</b> IMHO has one of the most angsty demonstrations of how an author can seamlessly annihilate a beloved character to epic proportions. <br/><br/>Dimitri and Rose were the two main reasons I loved Vampire Academy and half of that equation is now missing. What Mead did to Dimitri in Blood Promise and now Spirit Bound has me wondering if I</span>
  <span id="freeText17554750190816976721" style="display:none">Wow!!! Just wow!! I can now say with certainty that Vampire Academy has just become <i>the</i> classic example of why great books should not be allowed to become series. <b>Spirit Bound</b> IMHO has one of the most angsty demonstrations of how an author can seamlessly annihilate a beloved character to epic proportions. <br /><br />Dimitri and Rose were the two main reasons I loved Vampire Academy and half of that equation is now missing. What Mead did to Dimitri in Blood Promise and now Spirit Bound has me wondering if I'll ever be able to redeem him as a character.<br /><br />I have a tough time when characters in a book either physically or emotionally hurt or injure a protagonist that I've come to like, in this case Rose, and Dimitri has flawlessly done both to her. There was a time when I'd wave my <i>Save Team Dimitri</i> flag with pride and hope, but that flag is no more. If it wasn't sacrilegious to burn flags, I'd burn that one in a heartbeat. I just keep running in my head the hated lines of <i>I've given up on you. Love fades. Mine has.</i> Really?!!??!! After everything Rose did to try and save Dimtri that's what she gets and deserves? W.T.F.!! I don't care what mental monsters he's battling in his heart or head, you just don't say that to someone that not only loved you, but risked their life for you… time and time again.<br /><br />Most of my reviews include a smidge of a recap of the book. I just don't have the heart to revisit that just yet. <br /><br />In all fairness though, the book was written flawlessly, but at the same time the character annihilation was executed with precision. I am officially putting my Team Adrian shirt on and wearing it with pride. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3992876689522843917"><b>4/5</b><br/><br/>The 5th book in the series took me a little longer than I would have liked but I'm glad I was able to finish it. As a result, I don't remember every single thing that I was going to write in my review that I would have liked<br/><br/>One thing that I really liked was all of the plot twists. There were so many things that surprised me in this book and I was very glad for it. During the middle of the book however, I gotten a little bored. I kept going on though because I was (and still am) so interested </span>
  <span id="freeText3992876689522843917" style="display:none"><b>4/5</b><br /><br />The 5th book in the series took me a little longer than I would have liked but I'm glad I was able to finish it. As a result, I don't remember every single thing that I was going to write in my review that I would have liked<br /><br />One thing that I really liked was all of the plot twists. There were so many things that surprised me in this book and I was very glad for it. During the middle of the book however, I gotten a little bored. I kept going on though because I was (and still am) so interested about learning about Dimitri and how Rose is going to fix everything. I loved reading and learning more about the side characters such as Lissa and Christian and Adrean. The ending of this book was excellent and something that I am very excited about reading more in the 6th and final book.<br /><br />Overall this book was a little less than I expected but I did enjoy reading it.</span>
